best ergonomic fit with Word or other editing tools\r\n- Shadowed OCR text to easy identify the OCR's gaps in phrases\r\n- Tooltip for OCR-ed text to allow visual validation\r\n- Quick clipboard copy action button\r\n(* best results are obtained by using the proper OCR language selection)\r\n\r\n\r\nDocuments privacy \r\n\r\n- In memory processing\r\n- No external connectivity (no web service connections, no Cloud uploads, etc.)\r\n- No storage persistence (files and OCR results are not saved on the disk)\r\n- No special permission used/required (location, microphone, camera, etc.)\r\n\r\n\r\nUser notes\r\n\r\n- Although the application appears as Free+ in Windows Store, after the initial 3 days trial, the application requires an annual subscription add-on which is offering another supplementary 7 days trial period.\r\n- Specific languages (other than the default language) has to be installed in Windows 10 in order to be used by the application.\r\n- The trial period has no functional or feature limitations and no advertising appears during trial or subscription period\r\n\r\n\r\nQuickstart quide\r\n\r\n- Make a simple drag selection using the mouse (or touch) over the text to be recognized by OCR. search inside the document  \r\n- Click \"Rotate left\"/\"Rotate right\" buttons to change the current page orientation and reapply the
